# French Events

add_namespace = ww1_france

# France won but lose most of his manpower
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.64.t
	desc = ww1_france.64.d
	id = ww1_france.64
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_military_parade
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		has_country_flag = great_war_winner
		has_war = no
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 24
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.64.a
		trigger = {
			has_army_manpower = {
				size > 300000
			}
		}
		add_ideas = FRA_memory_of_the_somme
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.64.b
		trigger = {
			has_army_manpower = {
				size < 300000
			}
		}
		add_ideas = FRA_memory_of_the_somme2
	}
}

#France become socialist -> mention de censure focus
news_event = {
	title = ww1_france.41.t
	desc = ww1_france.41.desc
	id = ww1_france.41
	picture = ww1_france_41
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = socialist_france
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.41.a
		trigger = {
			tag = FRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = rule_superevent
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_ai = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = SE_fra_socialist
				play_song = "SE_fra_socialist"
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.41.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
			NOT = {
				tag = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = rule_superevent
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_ai = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = SE_fra_socialist
				play_song = "SE_fra_socialist"
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.41.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
				has_country_leader_ideology = social_democracy
				tag = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = rule_superevent
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_ai = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = SE_fra_socialist
				play_song = "SE_fra_socialist"
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.41.d
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader_ideology = social_democracy
			NOT = {
				tag = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = rule_superevent
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_ai = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = SE_fra_socialist
				play_song = "SE_fra_socialist"
			}
		}
	}
}

### new french legislative elections
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.43.t
	desc = ww1_france.43.d
	id = ww1_france.43
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		date > 1914.1.1
		has_elections = yes
		has_government = democratic
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = FRA_1914_elections_start
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = event_generic_ok
		set_country_flag = FRA_1914_elections_start
	}
}

####
#France lose his army, and is economy
####
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.48.t
	desc = ww1_france.48.d
	id = ww1_france.48
	picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_in_france
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		has_civil_war = no
		has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = GER
			has_war_with = AUS
			has_war_with = ITA
			has_war_with = ENG
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = achievement_france_surrender
		}
		has_country_flag = great_war_loser

	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = achievement_france_surrender
	}
	option = {
		name = event_generic_ok
		# this litteraly break interwar contents
		# FRA = {
		# 	country_event = {
		# 		id = ww1_france.307
		# 		days = 7
		# 	}
		# }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				ROOT = {
					delete_unit = {
						state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						arms_factory > 0
						is_owned_by = FRA
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 10
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						dockyard > 0
						is_owned_by = FRA
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 10
					}
				}
			}
			16 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 2
				}
			}
			14 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
				}
			}
			19 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
				}
			}
			19 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 2
				}
			}
			21 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 2
				}
			}
			add_ideas = FRA_land_army_restrictions
			add_ideas = FRA_naval_army_restrictions
			remove_ideas = idea_army_restrictions
			country_lock_all_division_template = yes
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			set_country_flag = dont_trigger_political_event
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_disband_army
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_disband_factories
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_military_restrictions_event
	}
}

# a communist uprising is coming
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.50.t
	desc = ww1_france.50.d
	id = ww1_france.50
	picture = GFX_report_event_spr_anarchist_uprising2
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_emergency_council
		has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
		has_country_flag = great_war_loser
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = FRA_surrender_alone
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.50.a
		set_country_flag = FRA_communist_uprising
		if = {
			limit = { has_stability > 0.10 }
			add_stability = -0.10
		}
	}
}

# Communard Sentiments in State
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.54.t
	desc = ww1_france.54.d
	id = ww1_france.54
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = event_generic_ok
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				is_on_continent = europe
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = communard_presence
				}
				any_neighbor_state = {
					has_state_flag = communard_presence
				}
			}
			set_state_flag = communard_presence
			custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_state_join_socialists
		}
	}
}

# Les Patriotes to protect the Old Regime
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.56.t
	desc = ww1_france.56.d
	id = ww1_france.56
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_parade_paris
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		has_country_flag = FRA_communist_civil_war_begun
		has_civil_war = yes
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.56.a
		division_template = {
			name = "Patriotes"
			priority = 0
			regiments = {
				militia = {
					x = 0
					y = 0
				}
				militia = {
					x = 0
					y = 1
				}
				militia = {
					x = 0
					y = 2
				}
			}
		}
		21 = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Patriotes\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
				owner = ROOT
			}
			create_unit = {

#assassination attemp on Jean Jaurès !
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.61.t
	desc = ww1_france.61.d
	id = ww1_france.61
	picture = GFX_ww1_france_61
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 150
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5 #150 days to 75 days to make it happen before the great war
			date > 1914.1.1
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		has_idea = FRA_jaures_in_danger
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		## he survived
		name = ww1_france.61.a
		remove_ideas = FRA_jaures_in_danger
		add_country_leader_trait = our_right_to_survive
		set_global_flag = Jaures_survived
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.61.b
		retire_character = FRA_jean_jaures
		FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = reformist_socialism
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = french_provisional_government
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = FRA_alexandre_millerand_pm_advisor
			add_ideas = FRA_alexandre_millerand
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_elections_post_jaures
		news_event = {
			id = kis_news.109
		}
		country_event = {
			days = 30
			id = ww1_france.62
		}
	}
}

	desc = ww1_france.62.d
	id = ww1_france.62
	picture = GFX_ww1_france_62
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

		name = ww1_france.62.a

			FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = reformist_socialism
				}
			}
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
		}
		promote_character = FRA_jean_longuet
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.62.b
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = reformist_socialism
				}
			}
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
		}

	}
}

# Jaures oppose to war
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.63.t
	desc = ww1_france.63.d
	id = ww1_france.63
	picture = GFX_ww1_france_63
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		has_country_leader = {
			character = FRA_jean_jaures
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_active_mission = european_crisis_mission
				has_guaranteed = SER
			}
			AND = {
				has_war_with = GER
				date < 1916.1.1
			}
			AND = {
				RUS = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_mobilization_flag
				}
				has_guaranteed = SER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.63.a
		FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = reformist_socialism
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = french_provisional_government
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_elections_post_jaures
		country_event = ww1_france.62
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.63.b
		if = { 
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = faction_traitor
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_guaranteed_by = ROOT
			}
			ROOT = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = betrayed_guarantee
			}
		}
		add_ideas = neutrality_idea
		add_ideas = civilian_economy
		set_country_flag = jaures_neutrality
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
				FRA = { white_peace = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_support > 0.90
			}
			add_stability = -0.90
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_support > 0.80
			}
			add_stability = -0.80
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_support > 0.70
			}
			add_stability = -0.70
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_support > 0.60
			}
			add_stability = -0.60
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.50
		}
		news_event = ww1_france.217
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}	
	}
}

#old guards officers retire if france is communist
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.68.t
	desc = ww1_france.68.d
	id = ww1_france.68
	picture = GFX_report_event_worried_french
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		has_government = communism
		has_war = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = fra_unit_leader_protests_socialism }
		any_unit_leader = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = old_guard
				has_trait = old_guard_navy
			}
		}	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 50
	}
	option = {
		name = event_generic_ok
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_unit_leader
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = old_guard
						has_trait = old_guard_navy
					}									
				}
				retire = yes			
			}
		}	
		set_country_flag = fra_unit_leader_protests_socialism
	}
}

				}
			}
		}

			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_rally_the_piou_piou	
				factor = 10000
			}
		}
	}

		trigger = {

			has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_rally_the_piou_piou
		}

		date < 1913.12.1
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = FRA_louis_barthou
			}
			has_country_flag = let_blum_stay_360_days
		}
		has_country_leader = {
			character = FRA_aristide_briand
		}
		has_elections = yes
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = FRA_gouvernement_provisoire
			}	
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 22
	}

		name = ww1_france.69.e

			long_name = FRA_democratic_party_long
			name = FRA_democratic_party 
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

# Louis Barthou retire 1913.12 (almost 1914) (Bored)
##################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.74
	title = ww1_france.73.t
	desc = ww1_france.73.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		has_government = democratic
		date > 1913.12.1
		date < 1914.6.1
		has_elections = yes
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = FRA_gouvernement_provisoire
			}
			has_country_flag = let_blum_stay_360_days	
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.69.f
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = FRA_gaston_doumergue
					}
					has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_rally_the_piou_piou
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_historical_pm_tt
		promote_character = FRA_gaston_doumergue
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.69.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = FRA_raymond_poincare
				}
				has_country_flag = FRA_raymond_poincare_elected
				has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_rally_the_piou_piou
				has_idea = FRA_raymond_poincare
			}
		}
		promote_character = FRA_raymond_poincare
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = democratic 
			long_name = FRA_democratic_party_long
			name = FRA_democratic_party 
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = FRA_ai_behavior 
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
					has_country_flag = FRA_AI_RANDOM_HISTORICAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FRA_ai_behavior 
						option = HISTORICAL
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.69.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = FRA_jules_pams
				}
				has_country_flag = FRA_jules_pams_elected
				has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_rally_the_piou_piou	
				has_idea = FRA_jules_pams
			}
		}
		promote_character = FRA_jules_pams
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = democratic 
			long_name = FRA_radical_party_long
			name = FRA_radical_party 
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = FRA_ai_behavior 
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
					has_country_flag = FRA_AI_RANDOM_HISTORICAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FRA_ai_behavior 
						option = HISTORICAL
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = FRA_aristide_briand
					}
					has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_rally_the_piou_piou
				}
			}
		}
		promote_character = FRA_aristide_briand

#
# arms safety review 
#
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.81
	title = ww1_france.81.t
	desc = ww1_france.81.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_balkan_pact
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		date > 1912.4.4
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = FRA_arms_safety_review
		}	
		has_start_date < 1914.6.14
	}																	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = FRA_arms_safety_review
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					set_variable = { islucky = 0 }
				}
				30 = {
					set_variable = { islucky = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#dont have any seat, maluses
		name = ww1_france.81.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FRA_arms_safety_regulation
			days = 180
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		#got 250 seats at least
		name = ww1_france.81.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				check_variable = {
					democrat_alliance > 250
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = FRA_250_seats
				}
			}
			check_variable = { islucky = 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_enough_seats
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_250_seats_with_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FRA_arms_safety_regulation
			days = 60
		}
	}
	option = {
		#got 150 seats at least
		name = ww1_france.81.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				check_variable = {
					democrat_alliance > 150
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = FRA_150_seats
				}
			}
			check_variable = { islucky = 1 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_enough_seats
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_150_seats_with_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FRA_arms_safety_regulation
			days = 60
		}
	}
	option = {
		#got 350 seats at least
		name = ww1_france.81.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 500
		}
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				check_variable = {
					democrat_alliance > 350
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = FRA_350_seats
				}
			}
			check_variable = { islucky = 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_enough_seats
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_350_seats_with_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		add_political_power = 10
	}

	option = {
		#got 350 seats at least
		name = ww1_france.81.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 500
		}
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				check_variable = {
					democrat_alliance > 250
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = FRA_250_seats
				}
			}
			check_variable = { islucky = 1 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_enough_seats
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_250_seats_with_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		custom_effect_tooltip = nothing_happend
	}
}

	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		date > 1911.7.7
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = FRA_bonnot_gang
		}	
		has_start_date < 1914.6.14
	}	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = FRA_bonnot_gang
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					set_variable = { islucky = 0 }
				}
				30 = {
					set_variable = { islucky = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#dont have any seat, maluses
		name = ww1_france.82.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		16 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = FRA
					industrial_complex > 1
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
				}
				add_state_modifier = {
					modifier = {
						local_manpower = -0.1
					}
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		#got 250 seats at least
		name = ww1_france.82.b
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				check_variable = {
					democrat_alliance > 250
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = FRA_250_seats
				}
			}
			check_variable = { islucky = 0 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_enough_seats
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_250_seats_with_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -1000
			producer = FRA
		}
	}
	option = {
		#got 150 seats at least
		name = ww1_france.82.b
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				check_variable = {
					democrat_alliance > 150
				}

				}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = line

		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_250_seats_with_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = line
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -1000
			producer = FRA
		}
	}

	option = {
		#got 350 seats at least
		name = ww1_france.82.c
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				check_variable = {
					democrat_alliance > 350
				}

				}

	title = ww1_france.83.t
	desc = ww1_france.83.d
	picture = GFX_ww1_france_83
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes																
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = FRA_THIRD_EMPIRE
			FRA_napoleon_v = {
				set_character_name = "Napoléon V"
				set_portraits = {
					civilian={
						large="gfx/leaders/FRA/FRA_Napoleon_V.png"
						small="gfx/interface/ideas/FRA/idea_FRA_napoleon.png"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		name = ww1_france.83.a
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		name = ww1_france.83.b
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.84
	title = ww1_france.84.t
	desc = ww1_france.84.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_france_parade
	is_triggered_only = yes																
	#We have no choice...
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.84.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				BEL = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FRA
					ratio < 2
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				BEL = {
					NOT = {
						is_guaranteed_by = GER
					}
					NOT = {
						is_guaranteed_by = ENG
					}
					NOT = {
						is_guaranteed_by = USA
					}
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				FRA = {
					is_in_faction = yes
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				threat > 0.25
				add = 1
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_france.85
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	# we refuse !
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.84.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				FRA = {
					has_war = yes
				}
				add = 10
			}

		}
		FRA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_france.86
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ww1_france.85
	title = ww1_france.85.t
	desc = ww1_france.85.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_peaceful_annexation
	is_triggered_only = yes																
	# victory
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.85.a
		FRA = {
			puppet = BEL
		}
		hidden_effect = { #so Flemish Nationalists don't rule pro-French Belgium
			BEL = {
				BEL_jules_jacques_de_dixmude = {
					promote_leader = yes
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
							traits = { ENG_haig_the_butcher war_industrialist }
						}
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism 
					name = BEL_army_party
					long_name = BEL_army_party
				}	
				set_cosmetic_tag = BEL_neutrality #otherwise it's called Greater Flanders
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ww1_france.98.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		is_in_faction_with = TUR
		is_subject = no
		is_faction_leader = no
		TUR = {
			is_subject = no
		}
	}	
	fire_only_once = yes
	#France must act
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.98.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
						is_in_faction_with = TUR
					}
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_france.99
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
	#We are fine with it
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.98.b
		add_political_power = -200
		add_stability = -0.10
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}
}

## French elections
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.234
	title = ww1_france.234.t
	desc = ww1_france.234.d
	picture = GFX_french_parliament
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		date > 1913.4.2
		date < 1914.1.1
		has_government = democratic	
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = FRA_1913_presidential_elections
		}
		has_elections = yes
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = FRA_1913_presidential_elections
			remove_french_presidents = yes
			clr_country_flag = FRA_raymond_poincare_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_jules_pams_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_edouard_vaillant_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_paul_deschanel_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_alexandre_millerand_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_gaston_doumergue_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_paul_painleve_elected
		}
	}
	option = {
		#raymond poincaré
		name = ww1_france.234.a
		trigger = {
			democratic > 0.30
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_historical_pm_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = FRA_raymond_poincare
				}
			}
			FRA_aristide_briand = {
				promote_character = yes
			}
		}
		add_ideas = FRA_raymond_poincare
		set_country_flag = FRA_raymond_poincare_elected
	}
	option = {
		#jules pams
		name = ww1_france.234.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_the_social_democrat_compromise
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
		add_ideas = FRA_jules_pams
		set_country_flag = FRA_jules_pams_elected
	}
	option = {
		#edouard vaillant
		name = ww1_france.234.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				or = {
					has_country_flag = FRA_AI_RANDOM_SOCIALIST
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FRA_ai_behavior
						option = SOCIALIST
					}
					has_country_flag = FRA_AI_RANDOM_SOCIALIST_REVOLUTIONNARY
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = FRA_ai_behavior
						option = SOCIALIST_REVOLUTIONNARY
					}
					has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_memories_of_the_commune
				}
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			communism > 0.30
		}
		add_ideas = FRA_edouard_vaillant
		set_country_flag = FRA_edouard_vaillant_elected
	}
}


#
# gaston calmette publishing evidences of caillaux corruption
# like foreign finance for campaigns / false justice in favor of criminals andc hidding infidely to his first spouse
# he also posted evidence that caillaux left depute is helping right wing politics by blocking an imposition law
# caillaux is furious
#
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.235
	title = ww1_france.235.t
	desc = ww1_france.235.d
	picture = GFX_caillaux_report
	trigger = {
		date > 1914.2.2
		has_start_date < 1914.6.14
		tag = FRA
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
			has_government = fascism
		}

		has_character = FRA_gaston_calmette
		has_character = FRA_joseph_caillaux
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = FRA_calilaux_affair
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = FRA_calilaux_affair
	}
	option = {
		##
		# Henriette caillaux kill gaston calmette
		# 20% change gaston calmette survive
		##
		random_list = {
			80 = {
				#gaston calmette died
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						days = 3
						id = ww1_france.236
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = fra_assassination_success
			}
			20 = {
				#gaston calmette survive
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						days = 3
						id = ww1_france.237
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = fra_assassination_fail
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.10
		name = ww1_france.235.a
	}
	option = {
		##
		# Caillaux pay a SFIO fanatic to kill calmette
		##
		name = ww1_france.235.b
		random_list = {
			80 = {
				#gaston calmette died
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						days = 3
						id = ww1_france.238
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = fra_assassination_success
			}
			20 = {
				#gaston calmette survive
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						days = 3
						id = ww1_france.239
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = fra_assassination_fail
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.10
	}
	option = {
		##
		# Caillaux and some of followers change side and join the opposition with high stability malus "the mask dropped"
		##
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = republicain_federation_allied
				has_country_flag = conservatives_allied
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			v = 7
		}
		name = ww1_france.235.c
		set_country_flag = FRA_caillaux_traitor
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_caillaux_traitor
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = lose
			value = 50
		}
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = lose
			min = 0
			max = radical_party
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = radical_party
			value = lose
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = conservatives
			value = lose
		}
		parliament_reassign_seats = yes
	}
}

# PACIFIST STRIKE
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.1
	title = ww1_france.1.t
	desc = ww1_france.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		has_government = democratic
		has_civil_war = no
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			any_country = {
				has_country_flag = FRA_nationalist_france_flag
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
			has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_memories_of_the_commune
		}
		AND = {
			has_stability < 0.05
			communism > 0.5
		}
	}
	# mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 2
	# }
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = french_pacifist_strikes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = FRA_idea_pacifist_strike
			add_ideas = FRA_interwar_Revanchism
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.1.a
		set_global_flag = french_provisional_government
		set_stability = 0.1
		set_war_support = 0.25
		FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
			promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = conservatism
				}
			}
		}
		suspend_elections = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 47
				neutrality = 8
				fascism = 2
				communism = 43
			}
		}
		add_ideas = FRA_idea_dual_power
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.1.b
		add_political_power = -150
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_france.4
			days = 21
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# SECOND PARIS COMMUNE
#########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.4
	title = ww1_france.4.t
	desc = ww1_france.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_government = democratic
		has_civil_war = no
		is_subject = no
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						has_army_size = {
							size < 24
						}
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Division d'Infanterie légère"
					is_locked = yes
					priority = 0

						infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
					}
				}
				19 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Garnison de Bordeaux\" division_template = \"Division de la gendarmerie nationale\" start_experience_factor = 0.7 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 9737
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
				31 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Garnison de Toulouse\" division_template = \"Division de la gendarmerie nationale\" start_experience_factor = 0.7 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 6766
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
				21 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Garnison de Marseille\" division_template = \"Division de la gendarmerie nationale\" start_experience_factor = 0.7 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 11834
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
				26 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Garnison de Vichy\" division_template = \"Division de la gendarmerie nationale\" start_experience_factor = 0.7 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 3594
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
				20 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Garnison de Lyon\" division_template = \"Division de la gendarmerie nationale\" start_experience_factor = 0.7 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 6613
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
				16 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Garnison de Paris\" division_template = \"Division de la gendarmerie nationale\" start_experience_factor = 1.0 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 9523
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
				30 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Garnison de Nantes\" division_template = \"Division de la gendarmerie nationale\" start_experience_factor = 1.0 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 11465
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = great_war_winner
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = PREV
						modifier = great_war_enemy
					}
					PREV = {
						add_opinion_modifier = {
							target = PREV
							modifier = great_war_enemy
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_stability = 0.54
			set_war_support = 0.75
			add_ideas = FRA_red_national_guards_cw
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					dismantle_faction = yes
					else = {
						leave_faction = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			FRA_pierre_monatte = {
				promote_character = yes
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = FRA_syndicalism_party_long
				name = FRA_syndicalism_party
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 16
				fascism = 11
				communism = 73
			}
			set_country_flag = FRA_socialist_france_flag
			load_focus_tree = france_socialist_focus
			set_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = FRA_fight_the_communists_title
				}
				set_country_flag = FRA_communist_civil_war_begun
				set_country_flag = WW1_demobilization
				add_ideas = FRA_disorganised_partisans
				add_ideas = interwar_recovery
				add_ideas = standing_alone
				# transfer_units_fraction = {
				# 	target = NFA
				# 	size = 0.6
				# 	keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				# 		NOT = {
				# 			is_character = FRA_maurice_sarrail
				# 			is_character = FRA_jacques_sadoul
				# 			has_trait = old_guard
				# 			has_trait = old_guard_navy
				# 			has_trait = politically_connected
				# 			has_trait = harsh_leader
				# 			has_trait = trait_royalist
				# 		}
				# 	}
				# }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = PREV
						NOT = { has_state_flag = communard_presence }
					}
					transfer_state_to = NFA
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = NFA
						has_state_flag = communard_presence
					}
					PREV = {
						set_state_owner = PREV
						set_state_controller = PREV
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Avant-garde socialiste"
					priority = 0
					regiments = { 
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { has_state_flag = communard_presence }
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Avant-garde socialiste\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 0.5"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = NFA
					size = 0.45
					stockpile_ratio = 0.1
					army_ratio = 0.45
					navy_ratio = 0.75
					air_ratio = 0.5
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
						OR = {
							is_character = FRA_maurice_sarrail
							is_character = FRA_jacques_sadoul
							NOT = {
								has_trait = old_guard
								has_trait = old_guard_navy
								has_trait = politically_connected
								has_trait = harsh_leader
								has_trait = trait_royalist
							}
						}
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Avant-garde socialiste"
					priority = 0
					regiments = {
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Avant-garde socialiste\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 0.5"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 2
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_subject = ALG
				}
				NFA = {
					annex_country = {
						target = ALG
					}
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = protectorate }
					clr_country_flag = protectorate
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_classic_blue }
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
				ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.5.a
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		set_global_flag = french_civil_war
		declare_war_on = {
			target = NFA
			type = civil_war
		}
		NFA = {
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.5.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = FRA_fight_the_communists_title }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = french_civil_war
		declare_war_on = {
			target = NFA
			type = civil_war
		}
	}
}

		tag = FRA

		date > 1924.6.1
		date < 1924.12.1

		has_elections = yes
	}

		days = 20
	}

			clr_country_flag = FRA_edouard_vaillant_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_paul_deschanel_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_alexandre_millerand_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_gaston_doumergue_elected
			clr_country_flag = FRA_paul_painleve_elected
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.17.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 6
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_historical_pm_tt
		add_ideas = FRA_gaston_doumergue
		set_country_flag = FRA_gaston_doumergue_elected
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_the_social_democrat_compromise
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
		add_ideas = FRA_paul_painleve
		set_country_flag = FRA_paul_painleve_elected
	}
}

	desc = ww1_france.18.d

			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			add_war_support = -0.02
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = rule_superevent
					option = DEFAULT
				}

			}
			hidden_effect = {
				play_song = "SE_fra_battle_of_verdun"
				set_country_flag = SE_battle_of_verdun
			}
		}
	}
}

#Italy seizes Savoy and Corsica

country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.22
	title = ww1_france.22.t
	desc = ww1_france.22.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
	}
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = great_war_ends
		tag = ITA
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			owns_state = 735
			owns_state = 1
			is_in_faction_with = FRA
		}
		FRA = {
			OR = {
				has_civil_war = yes
				any_country = {
					has_country_flag = FRA_nationalist_france_flag
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.22.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}
		ITA = {
			transfer_state = 735
			transfer_state = 834
			transfer_state = 1
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 661
					owns_state = 448
				}
				transfer_state = 458
				transfer_state = 665
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = FRA_nationalist_france_flag
			}
			NFA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_france.23
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.22.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.24
	title = ww1_france.24.t
	desc = ww1_france.24.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_ruins
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_state_core = 459
			set_capital = { state = 459 }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_on_continent = europe
					is_core_of = FRA
					NOT = { state = 1 }
				}
				set_state_owner_to = FRC
			}
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						original_tag = MLI
					}
				}
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
			# to fix weird desert mechanism
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 781
				}
				transfer_state = 515
				if = {
					limit = {
						567 = {
							owner = {
								NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_state = 567
					transfer_state = 775
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.24.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_capital = { state = 459 }
			white_peace = FRC
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

#Seizure of French colonies - except Indochine
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.25
	title = ww1_france.25.t
	desc = ww1_france.25.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_in_france
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		has_country_flag = great_war_loser
		OR = {
			has_civil_war = yes
			AND = {
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = FRA
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
				has_global_flag = french_civil_war
			}
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_on_continent = africa
				is_on_continent = north_america
				is_on_continent = south_america
				is_on_continent = australia
				is_on_continent = asia
				is_on_continent = middle_east
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.25.a
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = 83
					region = 179
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 737
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MOR
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 461
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 320
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 423
				}
				transfer_state = 320
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 812
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 273
				}
				transfer_state = 812
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_on_continent = africa
				NOT = {
					state = 774
					state = 969
					state = 1059
					region = 126
					region = 127
					region = 182
					region = 225
					region = 226
					is_core_of = MLI
					is_core_of = NGR
					is_core_of = IVO
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 539
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_on_continent = south_america
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 689
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_on_continent = north_america
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 331
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

# Interwar Entente
##########################################
news_event = {
	id = ww1_france.27
	title = ww1_france.27.t
	desc = ww1_france.27.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_french_parade
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = imperial_entente_formed
		NOT = { has_global_flag = interwar_entente_news }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	major = yes
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = interwar_entente_news
	}
	# For King and Country, return home!
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.27.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = has_british_monarchy
		}
	}
	# Break the chains!
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.27.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
	# Deutschland, stark, wachsam, bereit!
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.27.c
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
	}
	# Einigkeit macht stark
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.27.d
		trigger = {
			tag = AUS
			NOT = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
		}
	}
	# The legacy of the Weltkrieg
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.27.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = AUS
				has_country_flag = has_british_monarchy
				has_government = communism
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			}
		}
	}
	# Crush the syndicalist menace!
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.27.f
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
				has_country_flag = has_british_monarchy
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ww1_france.31.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		has_country_leader = {
			character = FRA_napoleon_v
		}
		date > 1926.5.1
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = FRA_napoleon_v
			clr_country_flag = alt_blue_tie_to_napoleon
			FRA_louis_joseph_bonaparte = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
						traits = { bonaparte_legacy_louis retired_minister_of_war }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.31.a
		FRA_louis_joseph_bonaparte = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
					traits = { bonaparte_legacy_louis retired_minister_of_war }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#Czechoslovak Legion
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.246
	title = ww1_france.246.t
	desc = ww1_france.246.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_czech_soldiers_02
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		has_character = FRA_milan_ratislav_stefanik
		is_subject = no
		# War is not over yet
		has_global_flag = great_war
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
			has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
			has_country_flag = FRA_czechoslovak_legion_flag
		}
		# Czechoslovakia is being oppressed
		any_other_country = {
			is_major = yes
			has_war_with = ROOT
			OR = {
				any_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = CZE
						is_core_of = SLO
					}
				}
				has_subject = CZE
				has_subject = SLO
			}
		}
		# Not in war with Czechoslovakia
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CZE
			}
			CZE = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SLO
			}
			SLO = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		date > 1916.1.1
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 365 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.246.a
		add_manpower = 9600
		effect_tooltip = {

# French Government collapsed
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.249
	title = ww1_france.249.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_france.249.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy_reserve
				has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_france.249.d2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy_reserve
				has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = ROOT
					popularity = -0.40
				}
			}
			remove_french_presidents = yes
			set_country_flag = FRA_parliament_dissolved
			# German backed social democratic interim government
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = communism }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 25
					communism = 27
					fascism = 35
					neutrality = 13
				}
				FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = social_democracy }				
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = social_democracy
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = FRA_republican_socialist_party_long
					name = FRA_republican_socialist_party
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism
			}
			# Monarch abdicated
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy_reserve
						has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.10
				}
				FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy_reserve }
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/FRA/FRA_regency_council_orlean.png" }
						}
						else = {
							set_portraits = {
								civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/FRA/FRA_regency_council_empire.png" }
							}
						}
					}
					set_character_name = FRA_regency_council
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = personalistic_dictatorship }
						promote_character = personalistic_dictatorship				
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = personalistic_dictatorship
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone
			}
			# German backed interim government
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.10
				}
				FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy				
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone	
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = FRA_neutrality_party
					name = FRA_neutrality_party
				}
			}
			# Falling republic government (default)
			else = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = -0.10
				}
				FRA_gouvernement_provisoire = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
						promote_character = conservatism
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = conservatism
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone	
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = FRA_democratic_party_long
					name = FRA_democratic_party
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = event_generic_ok
	}
}

#Franco-Syrian War Syria syrian conquest
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.256
	title = ww1_france.256.t
	desc = ww1_france.256.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_arab_revolt
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.256.a
		set_country_flag = franco_syrian_war
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SYR
			type = annex_everything
		}
		SYR = {
			add_ideas = standing_alone
		}
		activate_mission = FRA_syrian_conquest_timer
		hidden_effect = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Division d'infanterie stationnée à les TEO"
				priority = 0
				division_names_group = FRA_ARM_01
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					region = 228
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Division d'infanterie stationnée à les TEO\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
					owner = FRA
					count = 2
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = SYR }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

#Franco-Syrian War end
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.257
	title = ww1_france.257.t
	desc = ww1_france.257.d
	# fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_arab_revolt
	# trigger = {
	# 	tag = FRA
	# 	has_country_flag = franco_syrian_war
	# 	has_war = no
	# 	NOT = {
	# 		has_country_flag = franco_syrian_war_end
	# 	}
	# }
	# mean_time_to_happen = {
	# 	days = 2
	# }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SYR
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = SYR
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						exists = yes
						has_country_flag = great_war_winner
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 454
							state = 455
							state = 832
							state = 856
							state = 858
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = ENG
				}
				transfer_state = 852
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.257.a
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = -2
			name = san_remo_conference
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = ww1_france.261 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
}

						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				865 = {
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.15
			}
			AND = {
				17 = {
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				18 = {
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.15
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.25

		}
		
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.275.a #form a military governement around petains figure
		set_country_flag = FRA_collapsing_front
		unlock_decision_tooltip = FRA_petain_head_of_state
	}

#if France war end, democratic regime return
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.276
	title = ww1_france.276.t
	desc = ww1_france.276.d
	picture = GFX_petain
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		has_government = neutrality
		has_country_leader = {
			character = FRA_philippe_petain
		}
		has_country_flag = FRA_collapsing_front
		has_global_flag = great_war_ends
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = great_war_winner
			has_global_flag = FRA_surrender_alone
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = FRA_three_side_civil_war
			has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			has_country_flag = FRA_surrender_alone
			has_global_flag = FRA_surrender_alone
		}
		has_war = no
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.276.a
		FRA_philippe_petain = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = personalistic_dictatorship }
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = personalistic_dictatorship
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy }
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy_reserve }
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy_reserve
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = return_democratic
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.10
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_alt_blue }
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
				else = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = FRA_classic_blue
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = return_fascism
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.10
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Germany won against France... But just France
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.306.t
	desc = ww1_france.306.d
	id = ww1_france.306
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_parade_paris
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name =  ww1_france.306.a	# set up the truce ! 
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 500
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			FRA = {
				white_peace = GER
				add_ideas = standing_alone
				add_ideas = disarmed_nation
				add_ideas = interwar_recovery
				add_ideas = idea_armistice
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = has_capitulated_with_france_early
						}
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				ENG = {
					set_country_flag = entente_leader
					set_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = has_capitulated_with_france_early
							has_global_flag = russ_kapitulation
							tag = SOV
						}
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_country_flag = entente_leader
					set_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
						has_war_with = GER
						is_major = yes
						NOT = {
							tag = FRA
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = entente_leader
					set_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_subject_of = FRA
						original_tag = FRA
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = FRA_surrender_alone
				set_global_flag = FRA_surrender_alone
				set_country_flag = { flag = has_capitulated_with_france_early days = 180 value = 1 }
				leave_faction = yes
				add_ideas = standing_alone
				add_ideas = disarmed_nation
				add_ideas = interwar_recovery
				add_ideas = idea_armistice
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = FRA
							is_subject_of = FRA
						}
					}
					white_peace = PREV
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = PREV
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer_early
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = GER_mission_famine_timer_early
					days = 200
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
					days = 150
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FRA
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FRA
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FRA
					relation = docking_rights
					active = no
				}
				FRA = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = PREV
						relation = guarantee
						active = no
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = PREV
						relation = military_access
						active = no
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = PREV
						relation = docking_rights
						active = no
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
						is_subject_of = GER
						original_tag = GER
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = has_capitulated_with_france_early
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				remove_wargoal = {
					target = FRA
					type = all
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
							has_country_flag = has_capitulated_with_france_early
						}
						NOT = {
							OWNER = {
								is_in_faction_with = GER
								is_subject_of = GER
								has_war_together_with = GER
							}
						}
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = PREV
							is_core_of = PREV
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
							has_country_flag = has_capitulated_with_france_early
						}
						is_core_of = FRA
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_claimed_by = PREV
								is_core_of = PREV
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = FRA	## restitution of occupation zones in France
				}
				FRA = {
					give_military_access = PREV
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_france.306.tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = FRA
							is_subject_of = FRA
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = GER
						is_core_of = GER
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = GER
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_france.307
				days = 3
			}
		}

	}
}

	desc = ww1_france.307.d
	id = ww1_france.307
	picture = GFX_caillaux_report
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name =  ww1_france.307.a
		clr_global_flag = germany_accepts_FRA_capitulation
		clr_country_flag = entente_leader
		clr_country_flag = ask_for_peace
		add_ideas = FRA_interim_government
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		# What is the purpose of this? These are still French puppet and they lose their blue colours.
		# every_other_country = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		is_subject_of = ROOT
		# 		OR = {

		# 			tag = ALG
		# 			tag = TUN
		# 			tag = IND
		# 			tag = MLI
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# 	drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		# }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {	#petain shouldnt be able to stay if losed ww1, so stick authoritarian caillaux to monarchy ONLY
					has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
					has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy_reserve
				}
			}
			FRA_joseph_caillaux = {
				hidden_effect = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							traits = { corrupted_minister fra_homme_de_la_defaite }
						}
					}
				}
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = ww_one_trauma
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality < 0.30
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.30
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = FRA_interim_government_party
				name = FRA_interim_government_party
			}
			else = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
				}
				FRA_joseph_caillaux = {
					promote_character = social_liberalism
					add_country_leader_trait = fra_homme_de_la_defaite
				}
	
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_elections = yes }
			suspend_elections = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_french_presidents = yes
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_france.308
				days = 14
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_france.309
				days = 27
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_KINGDOM
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_KINGDOM_legitimist
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_THIRD_EMPIRE
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism_not_commune
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism_syndicalist
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism_republic_of
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = FRA_alt_blue
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA_remove_all_ideas = yes
		}
	}
}

### formation of FSN front du salut national
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.310.t
	desc = ww1_france.310.d
	id = ww1_france.310
	picture = report_event_damremont_manifestation
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name =  ww1_france.310.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.25
				}
			}
			FRA_philippe_petain = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = revolutionary_nationalism
					}
					promote_character = revolutionary_nationalism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = revolutionary_nationalism
							traits = { verdun_lion generallissimo }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_france.312
				days = 8
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = fascism
			name = FRA_FSN
			long_name = FRA_FSN_long
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			FRA_philippe_petain = { promote_character = stratocracy }
		}
	}
}

### France returns to War!
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.311
	title = ww1_france.311.t
	desc = ww1_france.311.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_france_parade
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = FRA_interim_government
			remove_ideas = idea_armistice
			remove_ideas = FRA_military_disloyalty
			remove_ideas = standing_alone
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.20
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = GER
					is_major = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV
						enemy = GER
					}
				}
			}
			FRA_joseph_caillaux = {
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = social_liberalism
				}
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = social_liberalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
						has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy_reserve
					}
				}
				FRA_maurice_pujo = {
					promote_character = personalistic_dictatorship
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = FRA_neutrality_party
					name = FRA_neutrality_party
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_KINGDOM
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_KINGDOM_legitimist
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_THIRD_EMPIRE
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism_not_commune
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism_syndicalist
						has_cosmetic_tag = FRA_socialism_republic_of
						# has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_authoritarian_coup
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = NFA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.311.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			remove_ideas = FRA_interim_government
			declare_war_on = {
				target = GER
				type = take_core_state
			}
		}
	}
}

### civil war placeholder for now
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.319.t
	desc = ww1_france.319.d
	id = ww1_france.319
	picture = GFX_french_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Partisans"
				is_locked = yes
				force_allow_recruiting = yes
				regiments = {
					irregular_infantry = {
						x = 0
						y = 0
					}
					irregular_infantry = {
						x = 0
						y = 1
					}
					irregular_infantry = {
						x = 0
						y = 2
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				
				FRA_create_FRC = yes
				FRC = {
					FRA_jean_longuet = {
						promote_character = yes
					}
					load_focus_tree = france_socialist_focus
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 15
							state = 16
							state = 30
							state = 14
							state = 785
							state = 24
							state = 29
							state = 865
						}
						is_controlled_by = FRA
					}
					transfer_state_to = FRC
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Partisans\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
						owner = FRC
					}
				}
				
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = FRC
					size = 0.30
					stockpile_ratio = 0.50
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
						NOT = {
							is_character = FRA_maurice_sarrail
							is_character = FRA_jacques_sadoul
						}	
						OR = {
							is_character = FRA_philippe_petain
							has_trait = old_guard
							has_trait = old_guard_navy
							has_trait = trait_royalist
							has_trait = war_hero
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				FRA_create_NFA = yes
				NFA = {
					FRA_ferdinand_foch = {
						promote_character = yes
					}
					load_focus_tree = france_nationalist_focus
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 31
							state = 22
							state = 26
							state = 25
							state = 19
							state = 23
							state = 33
						}
						is_controlled_by = FRA
					}
					transfer_state_to = NFA
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Partisans\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
						owner = NFA
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = FRA_classic_blue
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = NFA
					size = 0.45	#NFA has more soldiers
					stockpile_ratio = 0.45
					navy_ratio = 0.0 #but no navy
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
						NOT = {
							has_trait = old_guard
							has_trait = old_guard_navy
							has_trait = trait_royalist
						}
					}
				}
			}


			remove_ideas = FRA_interim_government
			remove_ideas = idea_armistice
			remove_ideas = FRA_military_disloyalty
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_on_continent = europe
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Partisans\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
					owner = FRA
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = FRA
						tag = NFA
						tag = FRC
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_france.320
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.319.a	 # democratic
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.319.b	# communist
		trigger = {
			FRC = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			FRC = {
				change_tag_from = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.319.c	# militarist
		trigger = {
			NFA = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			NFA = {
				change_tag_from = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

### civil war start
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.320.t
	desc = ww1_france.320.d
	id = ww1_france.320
	picture = GFX_french_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.320.a
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = FRA
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PREV
				type = civil_war
			}
			add_ideas = extensive_conscription
			add_ideas = partial_economic_mobilisation
			add_ideas = FRA_death_before_surrender
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = FRA_disjointed_government
				remove_ideas = FRA_disjointed_government2
				remove_ideas = FRA_disjointed_government3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			leave_faction = yes
			add_ideas = standing_alone
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FRA
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = FRA_unit_spawn_civil_war
					}
					FRA = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = NFA
							has_war_with = FRC
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = FRA_unit_spawn_civil_war
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 14
							state = 15
							state = 22
							state = 29
							state = 26
							state = 1
						}
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Partisans\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						owner = FRA
						count = 2
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FRC
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = FRC_unit_spawn_civil_war
					}
					FRC = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = NFA
							has_war_with = FRA
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = FRC_unit_spawn_civil_war
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 19
							state = 31
							state = 27
							state = 21
							state = 20
							state = 23

							state = 33
							state = 15
							state = 785
							state = 16
							state = 24
							state = 18
						}
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Partisans\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						owner = FRC
						count = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = NFA
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = NFA_unit_spawn_civil_war
					}
					NFA = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = FRC
							has_war_with = FRA
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = NFA_unit_spawn_civil_war
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 20
							state = 21
							state = 865
							state = 19
							state = 23
							state = 31
						}
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Partisans\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						owner = NFA
						count = 2
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						country_exists = NFA
					}
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = FRA_three_side_civil_war
					}
					FRA = {
						has_war_with = FRC
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 21
							state = 19
							state = 20
						}
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Partisans\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						owner = FRC
						count = 4
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = FRA_three_side_civil_war
		}
		
		
	}
}

### France accept deal
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.327.t
	desc = ww1_france.327.d
	id = ww1_france.327
	picture = GFX_french_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.327.a
		GER = {
			end_puppet = FRA
			set_autonomy = {
				target = FRA
				autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = FRA
					}
					FRA_victoire = {
						set_nationality = FRA
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = FRP
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = FRA_victoire
					}
					FRA_victoire = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_country_leader = yes
							}
							promote_character = personalistic_dictatorship
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = personalistic_dictatorship
									traits = { victoria_iii foreign_leader german_agent }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Victoria Louise"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/GER_Victoria_Louise.png"
							ideology = personalistic_dictatorship
							female = yes
							traits = {
								victoria_iii
								foreign_leader
								german_agent
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = GER_neutrality_party
				name = GER_neutrality_party
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_france.326
			days = 2
		}
	}
}

### War exhaustion for germany, war timeout
country_event = {
	title = ww1_france.330.t
	desc = ww1_france.330.d
	id = ww1_france.330
	picture = GFX_french_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		clr_global_flag = FRA_GER_intervention_button_pushed
		name = ww1_france.330.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = BEL
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = BEL
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
						}
						is_core_of = BEL
					}
					transfer_state_to = PREV
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				set_capital = { state = 6 }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRC
						is_in_faction_with = NFA
					}
					has_war_with = GER
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = PREV
						OR = {
							is_core_of = LUX
							is_core_of = FRA
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NFA = {
								exists = yes
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = NFA
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							FRC = {
								exists = yes
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = FRC
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = 16.OWNER
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				white_peace = 16.OWNER
				white_peace = 6.OWNER
				set_country_flag = failed_to_defeat_NFA_or_FRC_france
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ww1_france.331
	title = ww1_france.24.t
	desc = ww1_france.24.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_ruins
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.24.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = FRA
			}
			add_state_core = 459
			set_capital = { state = 459 }
			# to fix weird desert mechanism
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 567
				}
				transfer_state = 515
				transfer_state = 775
			}
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = NFA
					tag = FRC
					tag = FRA
				}
			}
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				transfer_state_to = PREV
			}
		}
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
				is_on_continent = europe
			}
			transfer_state_to = OWNER
		}
		random_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = FRA
			}
			ROOT = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_on_continent = europe
					}
					transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
				}
			}
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = FRA
					tag = FRC
					tag = NFA
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {

							NOT = {
								tag = MLI
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OWNER = {
					release = MLI
				}
			}
			556 = {
				add_core_of = MLI
			}
			news_event = ww1_france.336
			MLI = {
				add_ideas = MLI_disorganized_tribes
				add_ideas = standing_alone
				division_template = {
					name = "Militia"
					priority = 0
					regiments = {
						militia = {
							x = 0
							y = 0
						}
						militia = {
							x = 0
							y = 1
						}
						militia = {
							x = 0
							y = 2
						}
					}
				}
				556 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0 start_equipment_factor = 0.25"
						owner = MLI
						count = 5
					}
				}
				promote_character = MLI_dasa_marka
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Garnison en Afrique-Occidentale française"
				division_names_group = FRA_GAR_01
				priority = 0
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
			}
			272 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Garnison en Afrique-Occidentale française\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.75"
					owner = ROOT
					count = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		every_state = {

				is_owned_by = MLI
			}

		}

			target = MLI
			type = annex_everything
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.335.b	#huh no mali is too strong
		add_stability = -0.05
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_war_support < 0.20
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = MLI
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			# if we lost here, we are so damned
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = FRA_nationalist_france_flag
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.335.c	#play as mali ! Aw ka to Mali la!
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = MLI
