### Situation of French colonies
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.354
	title = ww1_france.354.t
	desc = ww1_france.354.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_french_parliament
	option = {	## we should release african republics
		# you can't just release mordern african republics there
		# and it is not sure that the tribes would just accept socialism there
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = SEN
				country_exists = RCG
			}
		}
		name = ww1_france.354.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						region = 140
						region = 226
						is_core_of = MRT
						is_core_of = MLI
						is_core_of = NGR
					}
				}
				add_core_of = SEN
				transfer_state_to = SEN
			}
			SEN = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = AOF
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						region = 183
						region = 184
						region = 227
						state = 775
					}
				}
				add_core_of = RCG
				transfer_state_to = RCG
			}
			RCG = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = AEF
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
				capital_scope = {
					is_on_continent = africa
				}
				OR = {
					tag = SEN
					tag = RCG
					is_subject_of = FRA
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 20
					neutrality = 14
					fascism = 0
					communism = 66
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = FRA_african_union_council
					picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/GER_workers_councils.png"
					ideology = reformist_socialism
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	## they must be integrated as part of france
		name = ww1_france.354.b
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = 140
					region = 226
					region = 183
					region = 184
					region = 227
					is_core_of = MRT
					is_core_of = MLI
					is_core_of = NGR
					state = 775
				}
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = FRA_french_integration
			}
		}
	}
}

#indochina, General Vuong Van Le march with rebel army
#The second figure who was seen by Vietnamese as a possible leader of an independent monarchy was Prince Cường Để
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.361
	title = ww1_france.361.t
	desc = ww1_france.361.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_saigon_streets
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = free_vietnam_fight
		}
	}	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = FRA
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = free_vietnam_fight 
					}
				}
				741 = {
					transfer_state_to = VIN
				}
				VIN = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = free_vietnam_fight
					VIN = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = IND
							type = civil_war
						}
					}
					VIN = {
						add_ideas = VIN_popular_mystic_army
						add_ideas = standing_alone
						division_template = {
							name = "Quang Phuc Quân"
							division_names_group = VIN_INF_01
							regiments = {
								militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							}
							is_locked = yes
						}
						741 = {
							create_unit = {
								division = "name = \"Su đoàn\" division_template = \"Quang Phuc Quân\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
								owner = PREV
								count = 3
							}
						}
						820 = {
							create_unit = {
								division = "name = \"Su đoàn\" division_template = \"Quang Phuc Quân\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.5"
								owner = PREV
								allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								count = 1
							}
						}
						286 = {
							create_unit = {
								division = "name = \"Su đoàn\" division_template = \"Quang Phuc Quân\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.5"
								owner = PREV
								allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								count = 2
							}
						}
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = VIN
						}
						add_claim_by = IND
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = free_vietnam_fight
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.361.a
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.361.b	
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}	
		VIN = {
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}

				id = ww1_france.370
				days = 2
			}
		}

				id = ww1_france.370
				days = 2
			}

			limit = {
				tag = FROM.OVERLORD
			}

			}

			}
		}

		}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.370
	title = ww1_france.370.t
	desc = ww1_france.370.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_saigon_streets
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.370.a
		# yes !
		if = {
			limit = {
				IND = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = SIA_railway_connection_done
					}
				}
			}
			IND = {
				build_railway = {
					path = { #bangkok to battambang to phnom penh
						10134 10177 7319 7376
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					build_railway = {
						path = { #bangkok to battambang to phnom penh
							10134 10177 7319 7376
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		IND = {
			set_country_flag = SIA_railway_connection_done
		}
		add_political_power = 25

	}
}

		}

			country_event = {

				days = 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {

			has_global_flag = great_war
		}
		NOT = {

		}
	}

	}

					limit = {

					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_philippe_petain

#Union sacrée crash !
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.426
	title = ww1_france.426.t
	desc = ww1_france.426.d
	trigger = {
		longest_war_length > 44
		has_war_with_major = yes
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		has_idea = FRA_idea_union_sacree
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_sfio_2
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.426.a
		remove_ideas = FRA_idea_union_sacree
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = ROOT
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.426.b
		#make concession -> prime minister blum
		trigger = {
			has_government = democratic
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = FRA_ww1_antagonize_sfio
				has_country_flag = FRA_law_against_far_left_leagues
				has_country_flag = FRA_anarchism_repression_law
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		FRA_leon_blum = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				promote_leader = yes	
				country_leader = {
					ideology = social_democracy
					traits = { moderate_socialist }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

		set_country_flag = has_ongoing_contract_with_FRA
		set_country_flag = FRA_is_buying_60_renault_tanks
		FRA = {
			set_country_flag = FRA_fulfill_mission_is_runing
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = FRA_60_tanks_contract_accepted
			value = 1
		}
		activate_decision = FRA_is_buying_60_renault_tanks
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_france.434
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA = {
				clr_country_flag = ongoing_contract_demand
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROM
					tag = USA
					tag = BEL
					tag = YUG
					tag = RUS
				}
				check_variable = {
					FRA_60_tanks_contract_accepted < 1
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				tag = POL
				check_variable = {
					FRA_60_tanks_contract_accepted < 2
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.431.b
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_france.435
				days = 1
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = has_refused_french_weapons
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA = {
				clr_country_flag = ongoing_contract_demand
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}

				OR = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ITA
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = FRA
					OWNER = {
						is_subject_of = FRA
						is_subject_of = ITA
					}
				}
				OR = {
					state = 21
					state = 834
					state = 998
					state = 158
				}
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = generic_local_investments
				days = 720
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_france.488
			days = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.487.b
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_france.489
			days = 2
		}
	}
}

#if you play socialist and your coalition breakout, you become democrat again
country_event = {
	id = ww1_france.528
	title = ww1_france.528.t
	desc = ww1_france.528.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		has_government = communism
		has_country_flag = player_coalition_is_minority
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = government_cant_be_replaced
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 24
	}
	picture = GFX_sfio_3
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.528.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		complete_national_focus = FRA_ww1_the_social_democrat_compromise
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = FRA_ww1_memories_of_the_commune
			uncomplete_children = no
		}
		add_ideas = FRA_disjointed_government
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = government_cant_be_replaced
				days = 280
				value = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					MOR = {
						is_subject_of = FRA
					}
				}
				MOR = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					set_cosmetic_tag = MOR_FRA
				}
			}
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			FRA_init_historical_loyalties = yes
			remove_ideas = FRA_defiant_army
			remove_ideas = FRA_CGT_support
			remove_ideas = FRA_CGT_support2
			remove_ideas = FRA_scientists_exodus
			remove_ideas = FRA_bourse_du_travail_paris
			if = {
				limit = {
					communism > 0.7
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.5
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							communism > 0.4
						}
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_france.528.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_you_reformed_the_high_command_and_have_high_popularity
		add_stability = -0.15
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_parliament_dissolved_tt
		set_country_flag = FRA_parliament_dissolved
		
		set_variable = { var = SFIO value = 600 } 
		set_variable = { var = independent_socialist value = 0 } 
		set_variable = { var = democratic_republican_alliance value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = radical_party value = 0 } 
		set_variable = { var = independent_radicals value = 0 } 
		set_variable = { var = republicain_federation value = 0 } 
		set_variable = { var = popular_liberal_action value = 0 } 
		set_variable = { var = nationalists value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = vacant value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = conservatives value = 0 }
		set_variable = { var = independent_republicans value = 0 }
		parliament_reassign_seats = yes
		set_variable = {
			democrat_alliance = 600 #issou
		}
		set_variable = { var = democrat_alliance_percent value = 100 } 
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 500
		}
	}
}
